# Module: Administration
Entities: 2, Associations: 1, Enumerations: 0
Flows: 8

## Domain Model
- ENTITY Administration.Account (persistent, generalization=System.User)
  - ATTR Email: StringAttributeType
  - ATTR FullName: StringAttributeType
  - ATTR IsLocalUser: BooleanAttributeType
- ENTITY Administration.AccountPasswordData (non-persistent)
  - ATTR ConfirmPassword: StringAttributeType
  - ATTR NewPassword: StringAttributeType
  - ATTR OldPassword: StringAttributeType
- ASSOC Administration.AccountPasswordData_Account: Administration.AccountPasswordData [*-1] Administration.Account

## Flows

FLOW Microflow: Administration.ChangeMyPassword
NODES=15; EDGES=13
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Account over association AccountPasswordData_Account from AccountPasswordData
3. ACTION JavaActionCallAction: call java action System.VerifyPassword -> OldPasswordOkay
4. DECISION Old password okay? expression=$OldPasswordOkay
5. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  6. ACTION ValidationFeedbackAction: ValidationFeedbackAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  7. END
8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  9. DECISION Passwords equal? expression=$AccountPasswordData/NewPassword = $AccountPasswordData/ConfirmPassword
  10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    11. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=The new passwords do not match., type=Error, blocking=true)
    12. END
  13. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    14. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Account (Password=$AccountPasswordData/NewPassword; refreshInClient=true)
    15. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=The password has been updated., type=Information, blocking=true)
    16. ACTION DeleteAction: delete AccountPasswordData (refreshInClient=false)
    17. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
    18. END

FLOW Microflow: Administration.ChangePassword
NODES=11; EDGES=9
1. START
2. DECISION Passwords equal? expression=$AccountPasswordData/NewPassword = $AccountPasswordData/ConfirmPassword
3. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  4. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=The new passwords do not match., type=Error, blocking=true)
  5. END
6. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  7. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Account over association AccountPasswordData_Account from AccountPasswordData
  8. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Account (Password=$AccountPasswordData/NewPassword; refreshInClient=true)
  9. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=The password has been updated., type=Information, blocking=true)
  10. ACTION DeleteAction: delete AccountPasswordData (refreshInClient=false)
  11. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
  12. END

FLOW Microflow: Administration.ManageMyAccount
NODES=8; EDGES=8
1. START
2. DECISION split currentUser
3. BRANCH when InheritanceCase=Administration.Account

  23. DECISION decision
  24. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=(empty)
    25. REF ExclusiveMerge
  26. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=NoInputParams
    27. REF ExclusiveMerge
  28. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=WrongNrOfInputParams
    29. REF ExclusiveMerge
  30. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=WrongReturnType
    31. REF ExclusiveMerge
  32. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=Valid
    33. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Column (Status=ExcelImporter.Status.VALID; refreshInClient=false)
    34. END
35. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=ValidReference
  36. REF ExclusiveMerge
37. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=UnUsed
  38. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
  39. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Column (Status=ExcelImporter.Status.INFO; refreshInClient=false)
  40. END
41. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=(empty)
  42. REF ExclusiveMerge

FLOW Microflow: ExcelImporter.SetupColumn
NODES=20; EDGES=14
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MxObjectType over association Template_MxObjectType from Template
3. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
4. ACTION ListOperationAction: ListOperationAction (output=Column, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
5. DECISION Found? expression=$Column != empty

  7. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow MxModelReflection.FindMember -> MxObjectMember
  8. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Column (Text=$Attribute, MappingType=ExcelImporter.MappingType.Attribute, IsKey=$IsKey, CaseSensitive=ExcelImporter.YesNo.Yes, DataSource=ExcelImporter.DataSource.CellValue, Column_Template=$Template, Column_MxObjectType=$Template/ExcelImporter.Template_MxObjectType, Column_MxObjectMember=$MxObjectMember; refreshInClient=false)
  9. DECISION has mf name? expression=$MFName != empty
  10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    11. END

    14. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Column (Column_Microflows=$Microflows; refreshInClient=false)
    15. END
16. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  17. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create ExcelImporter.Column as NewColumn (ColNumber=$ColNr)
  18. ACTION ChangeListAction: change ColumnList (type=Add, value=$NewColumn)
  19. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

FLOW Microflow: ExcelImporter.ValidateTemplate

        36. END
      37. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false

            53. END

            57. LOOP BODY

              69. DECISION Create everything? expression=$Reference/Handling = ExcelImporter.ReferenceHandlingEnum.CreateEverything
          70. REF ExclusiveMerge
      71. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        72. REF ExclusiveMerge
    73. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=SynchronizeOnlyExisting

    94. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true

      107. REF ExclusiveMerge

FLOW Microflow: ExcelImporter.Validate_TemplateDocument
NODES=13; EDGES=11

      9. END
    10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false

    15. END

  17. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=There is no excel document found for this template, type=Warning, blocking=true)

FLOW Rule: ExcelImporter.ValidateColumn
NODES=44; EDGES=41
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ObjectType over association Column_MxObjectType from Column
3. DECISION expression=$Column/MappingType
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=Reference
  5. DECISION has reference expression=$Column/ExcelImporter.Column_MxObjectReference != empty
  6. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    7. END
  8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    9. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Reference from MxModelReflection.MxObjectReference
    10. DECISION valid? expression=$Reference != empty
    11. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      12. END
    13. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      14. DECISION has objecttype expression=$Column/ExcelImporter.Column_MxObjectType_Reference != empty
      15. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        16. END
      17. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        18. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ObjectType_Ref from MxModelReflection.MxObjectType
        19. DECISION valid? expression=$Column/ExcelImporter.Column_MxObjectMember_Reference != empty and $ObjectType_Ref != empty
        20. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          21. END
        22. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
          23. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Members_Ref from MxModelReflection.MxObjectMember
          24. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=NrOfMembers_Ref, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
          25. DECISION > 0 expression=$NrOfMembers_Ref > 0
          26. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
            27. END
          28. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
            29. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MxObjectMember_Ref over association Column_MxObjectMember_Reference from Column
            30. DECISION Is the attr an auto number? expression=$MxObjectMember_Ref/AttributeTypeEnum = MxModelReflection.PrimitiveTypes.AutoNumber
            31. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
              32. END
            33. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
              34. DECISION Is attr Key expression=$Column/IsReferenceKey = ExcelImporter.ReferenceKeyType.YesMainAndAssociatedObject or $Column/IsReferenceKey = ExcelImpo...
              35. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
                36. DECISION Only search for objects? expression=$Template/ImportAction = ExcelImporter.ImportActions.SynchronizeOnlyExisting
                37. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
                  38. END
                39. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
                  40. END
              41. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
                42. END
43. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=Attribute
  44. DECISION has attribute expression=$Column/ExcelImporter.Column_MxObjectMember != empty
  45. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    46. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MemberList from MxModelReflection.MxObjectMember
    47. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=NrOfMembers, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    48. DECISION > 0 expression=$NrOfMembers > 0
    49. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      50. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MxObjectMember over association Column_MxObjectMember from Column
      51. DECISION Is the attr an auto number? expression=$MxObjectMember/AttributeTypeEnum = MxModelReflection.PrimitiveTypes.AutoNumber
      52. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        53. END
      54. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        55. DECISION Is attr Key expression=$Column/IsKey = ExcelImporter.YesNo.Yes
        56. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
          57. END
        58. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          59. DECISION Only search for objects? expression=$Template/ImportAction = ExcelImporter.ImportActions.SynchronizeOnlyExisting
          60. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
            61. END
          62. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
            63. END
    64. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      65. END
  66. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    67. END
68. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=DoNotUse
  69. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
  70. END
71. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=(empty)
  72. REF ExclusiveMerge

FLOW Rule: ExcelImporter.ValidateColumnMF
NODES=23; EDGES=21
1. START
2. DECISION has MF parser? expression=$Column/ExcelImporter.Column_Microflows != empty

    15. END

  19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true

    23. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Token (Status=MxModelReflection.Status.Invalid; refreshInClient=false)
    24. END

FLOW Microflow: MxModelReflection.IVK_RecalculateSize
NODES=5; EDGES=4
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve DbSizeEstimateList from MxModelReflection.DbSizeEstimate
3. LOOP iterate DbSizeEstimateList as Estimate
  4. LOOP BODY
    5. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MxObjectMemberList from MxModelReflection.MxObjectMember
    6. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=count, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    7. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Estimate (CalculatedSizeInBytes=$Size, CalculatedSizeInKiloBytes=ceil($Size : 1024); refreshInClient=false)
    8. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Size=8 + $count
    9. LOOP iterate MxObjectMemberList as Member
      10. LOOP BODY
        11. DECISION expression=$ValueType/TypeEnum
        12. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 1
        13. NODE ContinueEvent: ContinueEvent
        14. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 8
        15. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
        16. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 2+( ceil(if $Member/FieldLength != empty then $Member/FieldLength * 0.8 else 200) *2)
        17. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
        18. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 2+(20*2)
        19. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 2+(68*2)
        20. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 36
        21. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow MxModelReflection.Log -> LogProduct
        22. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ValueType over association MxObjectMember_Type from Member
        23. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 4
        24. DECISION has owner or changed by expression=contains( toLowerCase($Member/CompleteName), 'owner') or contains( toLowerCase($Member/CompleteName), 'changedby')
        25. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + ceil($LogProduct:8 )
        26. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
        27. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Size=$Size + 8
28. ACTION CommitAction: commit DbSizeEstimateList (refreshInClient=true, withEvents=true)
29. END

FLOW Microflow: MxModelReflection.Log
NODES=10; EDGES=8
1. START
2. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Product=1
3. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Comparator=$Base
4. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
5. DECISION Comparator = x expression=$Comparator >= $x
6. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  7. END
8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  9. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Comparator=$Comparator * $Base
  10. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Comparator=$Comparator * $Base
  11. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

5. END

FLOW Microflow: WorkflowCommons.ACT_Attachment_Save
NODES=14; EDGES=12
1. START
2. DECISION Has content? expression=$WorkflowAttachment/HasContents
3. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  4. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve WorkflowComment over association WorkflowAttachment_WorkflowComment from WorkflowAttachment
  5. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve WorkflowView over association WorkflowComment_WorkflowView from WorkflowComment
  6. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow WorkflowCommons.SUB_WorkflowView_CommentAttachment_Validate -> Valid
  7. DECISION Valid? expression=$Valid
  8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    9. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
    10. ACTION CommitAction: commit WorkflowAttachment (refreshInClient=true, withEvents=true)
    11. END
  12. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    13. ACTION DeleteAction: delete WorkflowAttachment (refreshInClient=true)
    14. END
15. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  16. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=Please upload an attachment., type=Warning, blocking=true)
  17. END

FLOW Microflow: WorkflowCommons.ACT_WorkflowDefinition_Delete
NODES=13; EDGES=11
1. START
2. DECISION Obsolete? expression=$WorkflowDefinition/IsObsolete
3. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  4. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve WorkflowList from System.Workflow
  5. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=WorkflowCount, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  6. DECISION = 0 expression=$WorkflowCount = 0
  7. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    8. ACTION DeleteAction: delete WorkflowDefinition (refreshInClient=true)
    9. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
    10. END
  11. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    12. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=This workflow definition still has instances. Use the clean-up instances function to delet..., type=Error, blocking=true)
    13. END
14. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  15. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=You can only delete a workflow definition when it is obsolete., type=Information, blocking=true)
  16. END

FLOW Microflow: WorkflowCommons.ACT_WorkflowDefinition_Lock
NODES=10; EDGES=9
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve WorkflowDefinition over association WorkflowDefinitionHelper_WorkflowDefinition from WorkflowDefinitionHelper
3. DECISION Pause instances? expression=$WorkflowDefinitionHelper/UpdateInstances
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  5. ACTION LockWorkflowAction: LockWorkflowAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  6. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
  7. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
  8. ACTION ShowPageAction: show page WorkflowCommons.WorkflowDefinition_ActionConfirmation
  9. END
10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  11. ACTION LockWorkflowAction: LockWorkflowAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  12. REF ExclusiveMerge

FLOW Microflow: WorkflowCommons.ACT_WorkflowDefinition_Unlock
NODES=10; EDGES=9
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve WorkflowDefinition over association WorkflowDefinitionHelper_WorkflowDefinition from WorkflowDefinitionHelper
3. DECISION Resume instances? expression=$WorkflowDefinitionHelper/UpdateInstances
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  5. ACTION UnlockWorkflowAction: UnlockWorkflowAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  6. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
  7. ACTION CloseFormAction: close page
  8. ACTION ShowPageAction: show page WorkflowCommons.WorkflowDefinition_ActionConfirmation
  9. END
10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  11. ACTION UnlockWorkflowAction: UnlockWorkflowAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  12. REF ExclusiveMerge

FLOW Nanoflow: WorkflowCommons.SUB_Duration_Calculate
NODES=20; EDGES=17
1. START
2. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create WorkflowCommons.DurationHelper as NewDurationHelper (Duration=empty)
3. DECISION Start? expression=$StartTime != empty
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  5. DECISION End? expression=$EndTime != empty
  6. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    7. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DurationInSeconds=ceil(secondsBetween($StartTime, $EndTime))
    8. DECISION Minutes? expression=$DurationInSeconds > 60
    9. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      10. DECISION Hours? expression=$DurationInSeconds > (60 * 60)
      11. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        12. DECISION Days? expression=$DurationInSeconds > (60 * 60 * 24)
        13. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
          14. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewDurationHelper (Duration=ceil($DurationInSeconds div (60 * 60 * 24)) + ' ' + getCaption(WorkflowCommons.Enum_DurationUnit.Days); refreshInClient=true)
          15. END
        16. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          17. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewDurationHelper (Duration=ceil($DurationInSeconds div (60 * 60)) + ' ' + getCaption(WorkflowCommons.Enum_DurationUnit.Hours); refreshInClient=true)
          18. END
      19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        20. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewDurationHelper (Duration=ceil($DurationInSeconds div 60) + ' ' + getCaption(WorkflowCommons.Enum_DurationUnit.Minutes); refreshInClient=true)
        21. END
    22. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      23. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewDurationHelper (Duration=$DurationInSeconds + ' ' + getCaption(WorkflowCommons.Enum_DurationUnit.Seconds); refreshInClient=true)
      24. END
  25. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    26. END
27. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  28. END
